 mri_label2label --srcsubject fsaverage --srclabel /gpfs/projects/adapt_lab/shared/TPOT/bids_data/derivatives/freesurfer/fsaverage/label/rh.BA1_exvivo.label --trgsubject sub-TPOT109 --trglabel ./rh.BA1_exvivo.label --hemi rh --regmethod surface 


srclabel = /gpfs/projects/adapt_lab/shared/TPOT/bids_data/derivatives/freesurfer/fsaverage/label/rh.BA1_exvivo.label

trgsubject = sub-TPOT109
trglabel = ./rh.BA1_exvivo.label
regmethod = surface

srchemi = rh
trghemi = rh
trgsurface = white
srcsurfreg = sphere.reg
trgsurfreg = sphere.reg
usehash = 1
Use ProjAbs  = 0, 0
Use ProjFrac = 0, 0
DoPaint 0
